OBJECT Report 11012732 Worksheet Service Order
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS14.00;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=[DEU=Arbeitsschein Serviceauftrag;
               ENU=Worksheet Service Order;
               NLD=Werkbon serviceorder;
               NOR=Arbeidsark, serviceordre;
               SVE=Kalkylblad ”ver serviceorder];
    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  CompanyInfo.GET;
                  FormatAddress.Company(CompanyAddress, CompanyInfo);
                END;

    OnPostReport=VAR
                   ServiceOrder@1100525001 : Record 11012823;
                   ServBudgetRec@1100525000 : Record 11012875;
                 BEGIN
                   IF (PrintCheckList) THEN BEGIN
                     IF PrintNextServiceOrders THEN
                       ServiceOrder.SETFILTER("No.", "Service Order".GETFILTER("Base Service Order No."))
                     ELSE
                       ServiceOrder.SETFILTER("No.", "Service Order".GETFILTER("No."));
                     REPORT.RUN(REPORT::"Service Order Inspection List", TRUE, FALSE, ServiceOrder);
                   END;

                   IF (PrintObjectSpecs) THEN BEGIN
                     IF PrintNextServiceOrders THEN
                       ServiceOrder.SETFILTER("No.", "Service Order".GETFILTER("Base Service Order No."))
                     ELSE
                       ServiceOrder.SETFILTER("No.", "Service Order".GETFILTER("No."));
                     REPORT.RUN(REPORT::"Service Order Object Specs.", TRUE, FALSE, ServiceOrder);
                   END;

                   IF (PrintBudgetLine) THEN BEGIN
                     ServBudgetRec.SETRANGE("Budget Type", ServBudgetRec."Budget Type"::Order);  //db, 17-12-07
                     IF PrintNextServiceOrders THEN
                       ServBudgetRec.SETFILTER("Service Order No.", "Service Order".GETFILTER("Base Service Order No."))
                     ELSE
                       ServBudgetRec.SETFILTER("Service Order No.", "Service Order".GETFILTER("No."));
                     REPORT.RUN(REPORT::"Service Order Budget Lines", TRUE, FALSE, ServBudgetRec);
                   END;
                 END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525004;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012823;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF (PrintNextServiceOrders) AND (GETFILTER("No.") <> '') THEN BEGIN
                                 SETFILTER("Base Service Order No.", GETFILTER("No."));
                                 SETRANGE("No.");
                               END;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  CustomerRec@1100525001 : Record 18;
                                  DocumentRec@1100525002 : Record 11012746;
                                  ServiceLocation@1100525003 : Record 11012801;
                                  DocumentLinkMgt@1100525005 : Codeunit 11012401;
                                  RecRef@1100525004 : RecordRef;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF (NOT CustomerRec.GET("Bill-to Customer No.")) THEN
                                    CustomerRec.INIT;
                                  FormatAddress.Customer(ServiceOrderInvoiceAddress, CustomerRec);

                                  CheckDimensionAddress("Global Dimension 1 Code");

                                  IF (NOT CurrReport.PREVIEW) THEN
                                    UpdateNoPrinted("No.");

                                  IF PrintDocuments THEN BEGIN
                                    DocumentRec.RESET;
                                    //db.sn, 01-08-14: C013460
                                    RecRef.GETTABLE("Service Order");
                                    DocumentLinkMgt.GetDocuments(DocumentRec, RecRef);

                                    ServiceOrderObject.SETRANGE("Service Order No.", "No.");
                                    IF ServiceOrderObject.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                      REPEAT
                                        IF ServiceObject.GET(ServiceOrderObject."Object No.") THEN BEGIN
                                          RecRef.GETTABLE(ServiceObject);
                                          DocumentLinkMgt.GetDocuments(DocumentRec, RecRef);
                                        END;
                                      UNTIL ServiceOrderObject.NEXT = 0;
                                    END;
                                    //db.en, 01-08-14: C013460

                                    IF ServiceLocation.GET("Service Location No.") THEN BEGIN
                                      RecRef.GETTABLE(ServiceLocation);
                                      DocumentLinkMgt.GetDocuments(DocumentRec, RecRef);
                                    END;

                                    DocumentRec.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
                                    IF DocumentRec.FINDSET(FALSE, FALSE) THEN BEGIN
                                      PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, DocumentRec);
                                    END;
                                    DocumentRec.CLEARMARKS();
                                  END;

                                  IF ("Base Service Order") THEN
                                    BaseOrderTxt := FIELDCAPTION("Base Service Order")
                                  ELSE
                                    BaseOrderTxt := '';
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No.,Service Contract No.,Service Location No.,Customer No. }

      ServiceOrderObject@1100409001 : Record 11071724;
      ServiceObject@1100409000 : Record 11071691;

    PROCEDURE UpdateNoPrinted@1210190000(INo@1210190000 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      lvServiceOrder@1210190001 : Record 11012823;
    BEGIN
      IF lvServiceOrder.GET(INo) THEN BEGIN
        lvServiceOrder."No. Printed" := lvServiceOrder."No. Printed" + 1;
        IF IncreaseStatus = TRUE THEN
          IF lvServiceOrder.Status < lvServiceOrder.Status::"In Process" THEN BEGIN
            lvServiceOrder.Status := lvServiceOrder.Status::"In Process";
            lvServiceOrder.HandleStatusChange; //mg, 06-05-2015: C023127
          END;
        lvServiceOrder.MODIFY;
        COMMIT;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckDimensionAddress@1100485005(Dim1Code@1100485003 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      ContactRec@1100485002 : Record 5050;
      DimValRec@1100485001 : Record 349;
      DimMgt@1100485000 : Codeunit 408;
    BEGIN
      IF (Dim1Code <> '') THEN BEGIN
        DimMgt.GetDimValueRec(1, Dim1Code, DimValRec, TRUE, '');
        IF (DimValRec."Contact No. (Company)" <> '') THEN BEGIN
          ContactRec.GET(DimValRec."Contact No. (Company)");
          FormatAddress.ContactAddr(CompanyAddress, ContactRec);
        END;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function



Shared offset as Integer
Shared newPage as Object

Public Function GetGroupPageNumber(PageCaption as Object, NewPage as Boolean, pagenumber as Integer) as Object
  If NewPage
    offset = pagenumber - 1
    NewPage = FALSE
  End If
  Return PageCaption &amp; " " &amp; pagenumber - offset
End Function

Public Function IsNewPage() as Boolean
  NewPage = TRUE
  Return NewPage
End Function

</Code>
  <Language>=User!Language</Language>
  <ConsumeContainerWhitespace>true</ConsumeContainerWhitespace>
  <rd:ReportUnitType>Cm</rd:ReportUnitType>
</Report>
    END_OF_RDLDATA
  }
}
